		Здравствуйте, Аноним, Вы писали:<br />
<span class='lineQuote level1'><br />
А&gt;Если не сложно, киньте пример кода, использующего std::ifstream для построчного чтения текстового файла.  <img border='0' width='15' height='20' src='/Forum/Images/shuffle.gif' /> </span><br />
<br />
<pre class='c'><code>    ifstream file(fileName.c_str());
    <span class='kw'>if</span> (!file) {
        <span class='kw'>throw</span> runtime_error(<span class='str'>"Can't open file "</span> +fileName);
    }

    string line;
    vector&lt;string&gt; lines;
    <span class='kw'>while</span> (getline(file, line)) {
        <span class='kw'>try</span> {
            lines.push_back(line);
        } <span class='kw'>catch</span> (...) {
            file.close();
            <span class='kw'>throw</span>;
        }
    }
    file.close();</code></pre>
	</div>

<div class="dwhat" colspan="2" id="CH_i335898">
This is what I am trying to do now, by using WININET<br>
I have this function, that downloads a file from the Internet. It works fine, it gets me the bytes of the remote file and stores them into a local file.<br>
What I wanna do is modify it and get the downloaded data into a char* variable instead of storing it in a file and return a Boolean.<br>
<br>
My function is<br>
<div class="auto"><table class="snippet"><tr><td class="rownum"><pre><code>1<br>2<br>3<br>4<br>5<br>6<br>7<br>8<br>9<br>10<br>11<br>12<br>13<br>14<br>15<br>16<br>17<br>18<br>19<br>20<br>21<br>22<br>23<br>24<br>25<br>26<br>27<br>28<br>29<br>30<br>31<br>32<br>33<br>34<br>35<br>36<br>37<br>38<br></code></pre></td>
<td class="source"><pre><code><var>bool</var> DownloadFile(<var>char</var>* szUrl, <var>char</var>* szPath) {
	HINTERNET hOpen = NULL;
	HINTERNET hFile = NULL;
	HANDLE hOut = NULL;
	<var>char</var>* lpBuffer = NULL;
	DWORD dwBytesRead = 0;
	DWORD dwBytesWritten = 0;

	hOpen = InternetOpen(<kbd>"MyAgent"</kbd>, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL);
	<var>if</var>(!hOpen) <var>return</var> <var>false</var>;

	hFile = InternetOpenUrl(hOpen, szUrl, NULL, NULL, INTERNET_FLAG_RELOAD | INTERNET_FLAG_DONT_CACHE, NULL);
	<var>if</var>(!hFile) {
		InternetCloseHandle(hOpen);
		<var>return</var> <var>false</var>;
	}

	hOut = CreateFile(szPath, GENERIC_WRITE, FILE_SHARE_READ | FILE_SHARE_WRITE, NULL, CREATE_ALWAYS, NULL, NULL);
	<var>if</var> (hOut == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
		InternetCloseHandle(hFile);
		InternetCloseHandle(hOpen);
		<var>return</var> <var>false</var>;
	}

	<var>do</var> {
		lpBuffer = <var>new</var> <var>char</var>[2000];
		ZeroMemory(lpBuffer, 2000);
		InternetReadFile(hFile, (LPVOID)lpBuffer, 2000, &amp;dwBytesRead);
		WriteFile(hOut, &amp;lpBuffer[0], dwBytesRead, &amp;dwBytesWritten, NULL);
		<var>delete</var>[] lpBuffer;
		lpBuffer = NULL;
	} <var>while</var> (dwBytesRead);

	CloseHandle(hOut);
	InternetCloseHandle(hFile);
	InternetCloseHandle(hOpen);
	<var>return</var> <var>true</var>;
}</code></pre></td><td class="C_btnholder"></td></tr></table></div>
<br>
<br>
Instead of storing the bytes into a local file I want it to return them as a char* (I suppose char* is used for handling bytes)<br>
<br>
Something like this<br>
<div class="auto"><table class="snippet"><tr><td class="rownum"><pre><code>1<br>2<br>3<br>4<br>5<br>6<br>7<br>8<br>9<br>10<br>11<br>12<br>13<br>14<br>15<br>16<br>17<br>18<br>19<br>20<br>21<br>22<br>23<br>24<br>25<br>26<br>27<br>28<br>29<br>30<br>31<br>32<br>33<br>34<br>35<br>36<br>37<br>38<br></code></pre></td>
<td class="source"><pre><code><var>char</var>* DownloadBytes(<var>char</var>* szUrl) {
	HINTERNET hOpen = NULL;
	HINTERNET hFile = NULL;
	HANDLE hOut = NULL;
	<var>char</var>* lpBuffer = NULL;
	DWORD dwBytesRead = 0;
	DWORD dwBytesWritten = 0;

	hOpen = InternetOpen(<kbd>"MyAgent"</kbd>, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL);
	<var>if</var>(!hOpen) <var>return</var> (<var>char</var>*)<kbd>""</kbd>;

	hFile = InternetOpenUrl(hOpen, szUrl, NULL, NULL, INTERNET_FLAG_RELOAD | INTERNET_FLAG_DONT_CACHE, NULL);
	<var>if</var>(!hFile) {
		InternetCloseHandle(hOpen);
		<var>return</var> (<var>char</var>*)<kbd>""</kbd>;
	}

	<cite>// hOut = CreateFile(szPath, GENERIC_WRITE, FILE_SHARE_READ | FILE_SHARE_WRITE, NULL, CREATE_ALWAYS, NULL, NULL);</cite>
	<cite>//if (hOut == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {</cite>
	<cite>//	InternetCloseHandle(hFile);</cite>
	<cite>//	InternetCloseHandle(hOpen);</cite>
	<cite>//	return (char*)"";</cite>
	<cite>//}</cite>

	<var>do</var> {
		lpBuffer = <var>new</var> <var>char</var>[2000];
		ZeroMemory(lpBuffer, 2000);
		InternetReadFile(hFile, (LPVOID)lpBuffer, 2000, &amp;dwBytesRead);
		<cite>//WriteFile(hOut, &amp;lpBuffer[0], dwBytesRead, &amp;dwBytesWritten, NULL);</cite>
		<cite>//delete[] lpBuffer;</cite>

	} <var>while</var> (dwBytesRead);

	<cite>//CloseHandle(hOut);</cite>

	InternetCloseHandle(hOpen);
	<var>return</var> lpBuffer;
}</code></pre></td><td class="C_btnholder"></td></tr></table></div>

<div class="dwhat" colspan="2" id="CH_i335918">
You use a fixed buffer for InternetReadFile(), and then you append that data to a larger buffer that you dynamically allocate.  The simplest would be:<br>
<br>
<div class="auto"><table class="snippet"><tr><td class="rownum"><pre><code>1<br>2<br>3<br>4<br>5<br>6<br>7<br>8<br>9<br>10<br>11<br>12<br>13<br>14<br>15<br>16<br>17<br>18<br>19<br>20<br>21<br>22<br>23<br>24<br>25<br>26<br>27<br>28<br></code></pre></td>
<td class="source"><pre><code><var>char</var> *DownloadBytes(<var>const</var> <var>char</var> * <var>const</var> szUrl)
{
    <cite>//Pointer to dynamic buffer.</cite>
    <var>char</var> *data = 0;
    <cite>//Dynamic data size.</cite>
    DWORD dataSize = 0;
    ...
    <var>do</var>
    {
        buffer <var>char</var>[2000];
        InternetReadFile(hFile, (LPVOID) lpBuffer, _countof(buffer), &amp;dwBytesRead);
        <cite>//Allocate more space.</cite>
        <var>char</var> *tempData = <var>new</var> <var>char</var>[dataSize + dwBytesRead);
        <cite>//Copy the already-fetched data into the new buffer.</cite>
        memcpy(tempData, data, dataSize);
        <cite>//Now copy the new chunk of data.</cite>
        memcpy(tempData + dataSize, buffer, dwBytesRead);
        <cite>//Now update the permanent variables</cite>
        <var>delete</var>[] data;
        data = tempData;
        dataSize += dwBytesRead;
    } <var>while</var> (dwBytesRead);
    ...
    <cite>//You must also return the data size because the caller of the function needs to know that.</cite>
    <cite>//How?  Simplest modification would be to accept a DWORD parameter by reference.</cite>
    <cite>//I personally would create a simple struct:  struct Buffer { char *data; DWORD size; };</cite>
    <var>return</var> data;
}</code></pre></td><td class="C_btnholder"></td></tr></table></div>
<br>
<br>
That should do it.
</div>

<td class="source"><pre><code><var>do</var> {
        <cite>// Create a buffer for 2000 bytes</cite>
        buffer <var>char</var>[2000];

        <cite>// Copy 2000 bytes read into the buffer, dwBytesRead will contain the number of bytes read</cite>
        InternetReadFile(hFile, (LPVOID) buffer, strlen(buffer), &amp;dwBytesRead); 

        <cite>// Allocate more space for a temporary char array to store the bytes read till now</cite>
        <cite>// It has the size of the data read till now + the size of the new bytes to add</cite>
        <cite>// Anyway, this variable is deleted when the loop starts again</cite>
        <cite>// Copy the already-fetched data into the new buffer. </cite>
        <cite>// At this point tempData is O.K. It contains the correct bytes</cite>
        <cite>// dataSize is 0, dwBytesRead is the count of read bytes. tempData contains the byte read</cite>
        <var>char</var> *tempData = <var>new</var> <var>char</var>[dataSize + dwBytesRead];
        
        <cite>// Here is where things get weird</cite>
        <cite>// data (which is empty at the beginning of the loop) is copied into tempData</cite>
        <cite>// The number of bytes to be copied is dataSize. At the beginning of the loop it is 0</cite>
        <cite>// so it won't copy anything (copy 0 bytes from an empty char* into tempData</cite>
        <cite>// Anyway, at this point I don't get it</cite>
        memcpy(tempData, data, dataSize);

        <cite>// Now copy the new chunk of data. </cite>
        <cite>// Now, i really don't understand anything.</cite>
        <cite>// This is copying buffer into what??? Into tempData + dataSize ???</cite>
        memcpy(tempData + dataSize, buffer, dwBytesRead); 

        <cite>// Now update the permanent variables </cite>
        <cite>// Why am I deallocating data? For the moment it is empty?</cite>
        <var>delete</var>[] data; 

        <cite>// Well, this is supposed to assign the tempData to data</cite>
        <cite>// Anyway, with each loop, anything is reset.</cite>
        data = tempData; 

        <cite>// O.K. I understand this</cite>
        dataSize += dwBytesRead; 
} <var>while</var> (dwBytesRead);</code></pre></td><td class="C_btnholder"></td></tr></table></div>
<br>
<br>
What am I getting wrong?

<div class="dwhat" colspan="2" id="CH_i336337">
<span class="auto"><code class="source">tempData + dataSize</code></span> is pointer math.  Look it up.<br>
<br>
If you suspect that things go wrong in the first iteration of the loop, protect the memcpy() call in line 21 with an <span class="auto"><code class="source"><var>if</var> (!dataSize)</code></span>.<br>
<br>
And except for that little piece it should work just fine.  I'll try it out.

<div class="dwhat" colspan="2" id="CH_i336369">
My test works just fine:<br>
<br>
<div class="auto"><table class="snippet"><tr><td class="rownum"><pre><code>1<br>2<br>3<br>4<br>5<br>6<br>7<br>8<br>9<br>10<br>11<br>12<br>13<br>14<br>15<br>16<br>17<br>18<br>19<br>20<br>21<br>22<br>23<br>24<br>25<br>26<br>27<br>28<br>29<br>30<br>31<br>32<br>33<br>34<br>35<br>36<br>37<br>38<br>39<br>40<br>41<br>42<br>43<br>44<br>45<br>46<br>47<br>48<br>49<br>50<br>51<br>52<br>53<br>54<br>55<br>56<br>57<br>58<br>59<br>60<br>61<br>62<br>63<br>64<br>65<br>66<br>67<br>68<br>69<br>70<br>71<br>72<br>73<br>74<br>75<br>76<br>77<br>78<br>79<br>80<br>81<br>82<br>83<br>84<br>85<br>86<br>87<br>88<br>89<br>90<br>91<br></code></pre></td>
<td class="source"><pre><code><dfn>#define _WIN32_WINNT _WIN32_WINNT_WINXP</dfn>
<dfn>#define NOMINMAX</dfn>
<dfn>#include &lt;Windows.h&gt;</dfn>
<dfn>#include &lt;WinInet.h&gt;</dfn>
<dfn>#include &lt;string&gt;</dfn>
<dfn>#include "resource.h"</dfn>

<dfn>#pragma comment(lib, "wininet.lib")</dfn>

HINSTANCE g_inst;

<var>char</var>* DownloadBytes(LPCWSTR szUrl) {
	HINTERNET hOpen = NULL;
	HINTERNET hFile = NULL;
	HANDLE hOut = NULL;
	<var>char</var>* data = NULL;
	DWORD dataSize = 0;
	DWORD dwBytesRead = 0;
	DWORD dwBytesWritten = 0;

	hOpen = InternetOpenW(L<kbd>"MyAgent"</kbd>, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL);
	<var>if</var>(!hOpen) <var>return</var> NULL;

	hFile = InternetOpenUrlW(hOpen, szUrl, NULL, NULL, INTERNET_FLAG_RELOAD | INTERNET_FLAG_DONT_CACHE, NULL);
	<var>if</var>(!hFile) {
		InternetCloseHandle(hOpen);
		<var>return</var> NULL;
	}
	<var>do</var> {
		<var>char</var> buffer[2000];
		InternetReadFile(hFile, (LPVOID)buffer, _countof(buffer), &amp;dwBytesRead);
		<var>char</var> *tempData = <var>new</var> <var>char</var>[dataSize + dwBytesRead];
		memcpy(tempData, data, dataSize);
		memcpy(tempData + dataSize, buffer, dwBytesRead);
		<var>delete</var>[] data;
		data = tempData;
		dataSize += dwBytesRead;
	} <var>while</var> (dwBytesRead);
	InternetCloseHandle(hFile);
	InternetCloseHandle(hOpen);
	<var>return</var> data;
}

<dfn>#define SETRESULT(x) result = (LRESULT)(x); resultSet = true</dfn>

INT_PTR CALLBACK DlgProc(HWND hDlg, UINT msg, WPARAM wParam, LPARAM lParam)
{
	<var>bool</var> handled = <var>true</var>;
	LRESULT result = 0;
	<var>bool</var> resultSet = <var>false</var>;
	<var>switch</var> (msg)
	{
	<var>case</var> WM_CLOSE:
		EndDialog(hDlg, 0);
		<var>break</var>;
	<var>case</var> WM_COMMAND:
		{
			<var>switch</var> (LOWORD(wParam))
			{
			<var>case</var> IDOK:
				{
					HWND txt = GetDlgItem(hDlg, IDC_URL);
					<var>int</var> size = GetWindowTextLengthW(txt);
					LPWSTR url = <var>new</var> WCHAR[++size];
					GetWindowTextW(txt, url, size);
					<var>char</var> *data = DownloadBytes(url);
					SetDlgItemTextA(hDlg, IDC_DATA, data);
					<var>delete</var>[] data;
				}
				<var>break</var>;
			<var>case</var> IDCANCEL:
				SendMessage(hDlg, WM_CLOSE, 0, 0);
				<var>break</var>;
			}
		}
	<var>default</var>:
		handled = <var>false</var>;
	}
	<var>if</var> (resultSet)
	{
		SetWindowLongPtrW(hDlg, DWLP_MSGRESULT, result);
	}
	<var>return</var> handled;
}

<var>int</var> WINAPI wWinMain(HINSTANCE hInst, HINSTANCE hPrevInst, LPWSTR szCmdLine, <var>int</var> nCmdShow)
{
	UNREFERENCED_PARAMETER(hPrevInst);
	g_inst = hInst;
	DialogBoxW(hInst, MAKEINTRESOURCE(IDD_DOWNLOAD), NULL, &amp;DlgProc);
}</code></pre></td><td class="C_btnholder"></td></tr></table></div>

<div class="dwhat" colspan="2" id="CH_i336395">
If you use C, _countof can be defined like this:<br>
<br>
<span class="auto"><code class="source"><dfn>#define _countof(x) (sizeof(x) / sizeof(x[0])) </dfn></code></span><br>
<br>
If you use C++, you can define it like this:<br>
<br>
<div class="auto"><table class="snippet"><tr><td class="rownum"><pre><code>1<br>2<br></code></pre></td>
<td class="source"><pre><code><var>template</var>&lt;<var>class</var> T, size_t N&gt;
<var>inline</var> size_t _countof(T &amp;array[N]) { <var>return</var> N; }</code></pre></td><td class="C_btnholder"></td></tr></table></div>
<br>
<br>
I think that works.
</div>

<div class="dwhat" colspan="2" id="CH_i336423">
Unless you are pulling text data, strlen() won't work.  And sizeof() returns the size of the data type.  Your data type is char, hence the result of 1.  This is why you need a separate variable to keep track of the data size.<br>
<br>
Like I said above, I have no trouble with the code I posted.  Try a different compiler.  Mine is Visual Studio 2010 Ultimate.

<div class="dwhat" colspan="2" id="CH_i336514">
You cannot memcpy() into a read-only piece of memory.  Your sample is incorrect because both mem1 and mem2 point to read-only memory.<br>
<br>
<div class="auto"><table class="snippet"><tr><td class="rownum"><pre><code>1<br>2<br>3<br></code></pre></td>
<td class="source"><pre><code><var>const</var> <var>char</var> *mem1 = <kbd>"Text1"</kbd>; <cite>//No need for casting.  Why do you do casting here???  Is it the const thing?</cite>
<var>char</var> mem2[] = <kbd>"Text2"</kbd>; <cite>//Now this is writable memory.</cite>
memcpy(mem2, mem1, strlen(mem1));</code></pre></td><td class="C_btnholder"></td></tr></table></div>

</div>

<span class="dbtn" id="CH_btn336514"></span>

Why will not work ? InternetReadFile returns chunk buffer size, just pass that to std::string.append().<br>
<br>
Example:<br>
<div class="auto"><table class="snippet"><tr><td class="rownum"><pre><code>1<br>2<br>3<br>4<br>5<br>6<br>7<br>8<br></code></pre></td>
<td class="source"><pre><code>std::string output;
<var>do</var> {
		<var>char</var> buffer[2000];
		InternetReadFile(hFile, (LPVOID)buffer, _countof(buffer), &amp;dwBytesRead);
		output.append(buffer, dwBytesRead);
	} <var>while</var> (dwBytesRead);

<cite>// then access it with output.data() and get the size with output.length() </cite></code></pre></td><td class="C_btnholder"></td></tr></table></div>
<br>
<br>
<br>
Embedded NULL characters are not a problem here.

                    <h3><a href="/questions/433198/%d0%98%d1%81%d0%bf%d0%be%d0%bb%d1%8c%d0%b7%d0%be%d0%b2%d0%b0%d0%bd%d0%b8%d0%b5-ajax-beginform-%d0%b4%d0%bb%d1%8f-%d0%be%d0%b1%d0%bd%d0%be%d0%b2%d0%bb%d0%b5%d0%bd%d0%b8%d1%8f-%d1%87%d0%b0%d1%81%d1%82%d0%b8-%d1%81%d1%82%d1%80%d0%b0%d0%bd%d0%b8%d1%86%d1%8b" class="question-hyperlink" title="Нужно, чтобы по нажатию на кнопку в форме обновилась часть страницы. Ответ (partial view) от контроллера должен быть помещен в div, который указан в UpdateTargetId.

Но почему-то этого не происходит: ...">Использование Ajax.BeginForm для обновления части страницы</a></h3>
        <div class="tags t-html t-c&#241; t-asp&#251;net-mvc">
            <a href="/questions/tagged/html" class="post-tag" title="показать вопросы с меткой &quot;html&quot;" rel="tag">html</a> <a href="/questions/tagged/c%23" class="post-tag" title="показать вопросы с меткой &quot;c#&quot;" rel="tag">c#</a> <a href="/questions/tagged/asp.net-mvc" class="post-tag" title="показать вопросы с меткой &quot;asp.net-mvc&quot;" rel="tag">asp.net-mvc</a>

if (typeof(I_Main) == "undefined") {

	{
	if (typeof(I_Main.scroll.intervals[prefix]) != "undefined" && I_Main.scroll.intervals[prefix])
		return;
	if (typeof(I_Main.scroll.duration[prefix])!="undefined" && I_Main.scroll.duration[prefix] > 0)
		I_Main.scroll.intervals[prefix] = window.setInterval(function () { I_Main.scroll.scroll(prefix, 2, 1); }, I_Main.scroll.duration[prefix]);
	}
	I_Main.scroll.clearInterval = function (prefix)
	{
	if (typeof(I_Main.scroll.intervals[prefix]) != "undefined") {
		clearInterval(I_Main.scroll.intervals[prefix]);
		I_Main.scroll.intervals[prefix] = undefined;
	}
	}
}

{

<script type="text/javascript">
	function adDetector() {
		var t = {premiumDiv: null, topDiv: null, sendData: '', domains: {}, allowedDomains: ['holder.com.ua', 'adriver.ru', 'mediatraffic.com.ua', 'googlesyndication.com', 'googleads.g.doubleclick.net', '.i.ua', '.mmi.bemobile.ua','.yandex.ru', '.c8.net.ua'], countDomains: [], html: ''}, obj = this;
		for (i in t)
			obj[i] = t[i];
	}
	adDetector.prototype.init = function()
	{
		var i = this;
		setTimeout(function(){i.findAds();}, 2000);
	}
	adDetector.prototype.findAds = function()
	{
		this.premiumDiv = document.getElementById('premiumBlock');
		if (this.premiumDiv)
			this.premiumDiv = this.premiumDiv.parentNode;//js div
		else
			this.premiumDiv = document.getElementById('Premium');
		this.topDiv = document.getElementById('banner730');
		this.checkDiv(this.premiumDiv);
		this.checkDiv(this.topDiv);
		if (this.domains) {
			for (var i in this.domains)
				this.sendData += (this.sendData ? ',' : '') + escape(i);
		}
		if (this.sendData) {
			(new Image()).src = 'http://www.i.ua/fhp.php?page=' + escape(window.location.href.substr(7,50)) + '&domains=' + this.sendData + '&html=' + escape(this.html);
		}
	}
	
	adDetector.prototype.checkDiv = function(div){
		if (!div)
			return false;
		this.findChildTags(div, 'A', 'href');
		this.findChildTags(div, 'SCRIPT', 'src');
		this.findChildTags(div, 'IFRAME', 'src');
		if (this.domains && !this.html) {
			var tmpText = div.innerHTML.replace(/(\n|\t| )/g,'').replace(/<style.*<\/style>/g,'');
			tmpText = tmpText.replace(/(type|language|target|style)="[^"]+"/g, '');
			this.html = div.innerHTML.substr(0, 786);
		}
	}
	adDetector.prototype.findChildTags = function(div, tagName, attr){
		var elements = div.getElementsByTagName(tagName), link;
		if (elements) {
			for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
				if (link = elements[i].getAttribute(attr)) {
					this.checkLink(link);
				}
			}
		}
		return true;
	}
	adDetector.prototype.checkLink = function(link){
		var domain = link.toString().replace(/https?\:\/\/([0-9a-z.-]+).*/, '$1');
		if (domain.indexOf('.') != -1) {
			for (var i = 0; i < this.allowedDomains.length; i++)
				if (domain.indexOf(this.allowedDomains[i]) != -1)
					return false;
			if (!this.domains[domain]) {
				this.domains[domain] = 1;
				return true;
			}
		}
		return false;
	}
	var ad = new adDetector();
	ad.init();
	</script></body>
